				}
			}

			}
		}

				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = zoroastrian_great_fire_warriors
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		if = {

				event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_farmers = {

				}
			}
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = zoroastrian_great_fire_farmers
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
			}
			add_nationalism = -4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
			}
			add_nationalism = -3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
			}
			add_nationalism = -2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
			}
			add_nationalism = -1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					religion = zoroastrian
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = zoroastrian_10
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = {
					which = zoroastrian
					value = 2
				}
				change_variable = {
					which = province_religion
					value = -2
				}
			}
		}
		owner = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
				add_prestige = 5
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
				add_prestige = 4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				add_prestige = 3
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				add_prestige = 2
			}
			else = {
				add_prestige = 1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
				add_legitimacy = 2.5
				add_devotion = 5
				add_republican_tradition = 1.25
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
				add_legitimacy = 2
				add_devotion = 4
				add_republican_tradition = 1
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				add_legitimacy = 1.5
				add_devotion = 3
				add_republican_tradition = 0.75
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				add_legitimacy = 1
				add_devotion = 2
				add_republican_tradition = 0.5
			}
			else = {
				add_legitimacy = 0.5
				add_devotion = 1
				add_republican_tradition = 0.25
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_priests = {
					owner = {
						NOT = {
							religion = zoroastrian
						}
					}
				}
			}
			event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_priests = {
				add_claim = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_warriors = {
					owner = {
						NOT = {
							religion = zoroastrian
						}
					}
				}
			}
			event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_warriors = {
				add_claim = PREV
			}
		}
		if = {

						}
					}
				}
			}

country_event = {
	id = dg_zoroastrian.045
	title = dg_zoroastrian.045.t
	desc = dg_zoroastrian.045.d
	picture = zoroastrian_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					num_of_generals = 2
					NOT = {
						has_advisor = yes
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = dg_zoroastrian.045.general
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						num_of_generals = 2
						NOT = {
							has_advisor = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = dg_zoroastrian.045.advisor
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_zoroastrian.045.dismiss
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					num_of_generals = 2
					NOT = {
						has_advisor = yes
					}
				}
			}
			kill_leader = {
				type = random
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					OR = {
						num_of_generals = 2
						NOT = {
							has_advisor = yes
						}
					}
				}
			}
			kill_advisor = random
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_zoroastrian.045.defend
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				monthly_income = 4.2
			}
			add_years_of_income = -0.10
		}
		else = {
			add_treasury = -5
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.60
			}
			add_legitimacy = 5
			add_devotion = 10
			add_republican_tradition = 2.5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.20
			}
			add_legitimacy = 4
			add_devotion = 8
			add_republican_tradition = 2
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.20
			}
			add_legitimacy = 3
			add_devotion = 6
			add_republican_tradition = 1.5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.60
			}
			add_legitimacy = 2
			add_devotion = 4
			add_republican_tradition = 1
		}
		else = {
			add_legitimacy = 1
			add_devotion = 2
			add_republican_tradition = 0.5
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_zoroastrian.045.ignore
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.20
				factor = 0.7
			}
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.60
				factor = 0.7
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = dg_zoroastrian.046
	title = dg_zoroastrian.046.t
	desc = dg_zoroastrian.046.d
	picture = zoroastrian_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = zoroastrian_priesthood_reestablished
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = dg_zoroastrian.046.d_no_patriarch
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = patriarch_corrupt
					has_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = dg_zoroastrian.046.d_patriarch
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_zoroastrian.046.patriarch
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = zoroastrian_priesthood_reestablished
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = patriarch_corrupt
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_powerful
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_strong
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_moderate
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_weak
			}
			NOT = {
				has_country_modifier = unhappy_church_impotent
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		add_dip_power = -5
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
			}
			random = {
				chance = 30
				custom_tooltip = patriarch_becomes_hostile
				clr_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
				set_country_flag = patriarch_controversial
				clr_country_flag = patriarch_zealous

	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = zoroastrian_priesthood_reestablished
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_modifier = caste_system_relaxed
					}
					NOT = {
						has_country_modifier = caste_system_loose
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = dg_zoroastrian.047.d_2
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_modifier = caste_system_relaxed
						has_country_modifier = caste_system_loose
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = dg_zoroastrian.047.d_3
			}
		}
		else = {
			custom_tooltip = dg_zoroastrian.047.d_1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_zoroastrian.047.accept
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 20
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = preacher_shortage
			duration = 5000
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_zoroastrian.047.lower_standards
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				factor = 2
			}
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.20
				factor = 0.5
			}
			modifier = {
				piety = 0.60
				factor = 0.5
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.60
			}
			add_prestige = -5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.20
			}
			add_prestige = -4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.20
			}
			add_prestige = -3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.60
			}
			add_prestige = -2
		}
		else = {
			add_prestige = -1
		}
		add_piety = -0.20
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = impious_priests
			duration = 5000
			hidden = yes
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_zoroastrian.047.dastur
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = caste_system_relaxed
				has_country_modifier = caste_system_loose
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50
		}
		add_adm_power = -5
	}
}

	id = dg_zoroastrian.061
	title = dg_zoroastrian.061.t
	desc = dg_zoroastrian.061.d
	picture = zoroastrian_religion
	trigger = {
		ai = no
		AND = {
			culture_group = persian_group
		}
		check_variable = {
			which = zoroastrian_population
			value = 10
		}
		NOT = {
			has_global_flag = zoroastrian_sassanid_gambit
		}
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				stability = 1
			}
			num_of_revolts = 1
			NOT = {
				legitimacy = 90
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			religion = zoroastrian
		}
		NOT = {
			government = theocracy
		}
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		years = 20
	}

		set_global_flag = zoroastrian_sassanid_gambit
	}

		name = dg_zoroastrian.061.no
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
		}
	}

		name = dg_zoroastrian.061.yes
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 0
		}

			limit = {
				AND = {
					culture_group = persian_group

				}

					OR = {
						continent = southeast_asia

		if = {
			limit = {
				advisor = theologian
			}
			custom_tooltip = convert_theologian
			custom_tooltip = stability_points_gained_50
			hidden_effect = {
				change_variable = {
					which = stability_points
					value = 50
				}
				country_event = {
					id = POP_Stability.002
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = was_zoroastrian
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = sympathy_to_old_religion
						value = 1
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = convert_previous_recent
				custom_tooltip = stability_points_gained_100
				hidden_effect = {
					change_variable = {
						which = stability_points
						value = 100
					}
					country_event = {
						id = POP_Stability.002
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = convert_previous_old
				custom_tooltip = stability_points_gained_50
				hidden_effect = {
					change_variable = {
						which = stability_points
						value = 50
					}
					country_event = {
						id = POP_Stability.002
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = sympathy_to_old_religion
						value = 1
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = convert_recent
				custom_tooltip = stability_points_gained_50
				hidden_effect = {
					change_variable = {
						which = stability_points
						value = 50
					}
					country_event = {
						id = POP_Stability.002
					}
				}
			}
		}
		change_religion = zoroastrian
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = dg_zoroastrian.062
	title = dg_zoroastrian.062.t
	desc = dg_zoroastrian.062.d
	picture = zoroastrian_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = zoroastrian_avestas_restored
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = zoroastrian_revival
		}
	}
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						culture_group = persian_group
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = dg_zoroastrian.062.return
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_zoroastrian.062.only
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = zoroastrian_revival
			}
			NOT = {
				any_known_country = {
					religion = zoroastrian
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = zoroastrian_revival
		if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.60
			}
			add_prestige = 5
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.20
			}
			add_prestige = 4
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.20
			}
			add_prestige = 3
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.60
			}
			add_prestige = 2
		}
		else = {
			add_prestige = 1
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						culture_group = persian_group
					}
				}
			}
			every_province = {
				limit = {
					religion = zoroastrian
					AND = {
						culture_group = persian_group
					}
					NOT = {
						owned_by = ROOT
					}
					NOT = {
						owner = {
							overlord_of = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				add_claim = ROOT
			}
		}
		every_known_country = {
			limit = {
				any_owned_province = {
					OR = {
						religion = zoroastrian
						check_variable = {
							which = zoroastrian
							value = 2
						}
					}
				}
				NOT = {
					religion = zoroastrian
				}
				NOT = {
					zoroastrian = 2
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = dg_zoroastrian.063
				days = 30
				random = 180
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_priests = {
					owner = {
						NOT = {
							religion = zoroastrian
						}
					}
				}
			}
			event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_priests = {
				add_claim = ROOT
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_warriors = {
					owner = {
						NOT = {
							religion = zoroastrian
						}
					}
				}
			}
			event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_warriors = {
				add_claim = PREV
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_farmers = {
					owner = {
						NOT = {
							religion = zoroastrian
						}
					}
				}
			}
			event_target:zoroastrian_great_fire_farmers = {
				add_claim = PREV
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_zoroastrian.062.notonly
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = zoroastrian_revival
				any_known_country = {
					religion = zoroastrian
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = zoroastrian_revival
	}
}

		set_country_flag = zoroastrian_avestas_modern_scripture
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = zoroastrian_avestas_progressive_reform
			duration = 5000
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			change_variable = {
				which = zoroastrian_avestas_progressive
				value = 1
			}
			change_variable = {
				which = zoroastrian_avestas_traditionalist
				value = 0.25
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = zoroastrian_avestas_islam
					has_country_flag = zoroastrian_avestas_philosophy
					has_country_flag = zoroastrian_avestas_polytheism
					has_country_flag = zoroastrian_avestas_language
				}
				country_event = {
					id = dg_zoroastrian.069
					days = 0
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = dg_zoroastrian.069
	title = dg_zoroastrian.069.t
	desc = dg_zoroastrian.069.d
	picture = zoroastrian_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = zoroastrianism_reformed
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = zoroastrian_avestas_traditionalist
					which = zoroastrian_avestas_restorationist
				}
				check_variable = {
					which = zoroastrian_avestas_traditionalist
					which = zoroastrian_avestas_progressive
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = traditionalist_zoroastrianism
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							which = zoroastrian_avestas_traditionalist
							which = zoroastrian_avestas_restorationist
						}
					}
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							which = zoroastrian_avestas_traditionalist
							which = zoroastrian_avestas_progressive
						}
					}
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = {
						which = zoroastrian_avestas_restorationist
						which = zoroastrian_avestas_progressive
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = restorationist_zoroastrianism
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						check_variable = {
							which = zoroastrian_avestas_restorationist
							which = zoroastrian_avestas_progressive
						}
					}
				}
				set_country_flag = progressive_zoroastrianism
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				which = zoroastrian_avestas_restorationist
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = zoroastrian_avestas_traditionalist
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = zoroastrian_avestas_progressive
				value = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_zoroastrian.069.a
		remove_country_modifier = fragmented_scriptures
		if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.60
			}
			add_prestige = 15
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.20
			}
			add_prestige = 12
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.20
			}
			add_prestige = 9
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.60
			}
			add_prestige = 6
		}
		else = {
			add_prestige = 3
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = traditionalist_zoroastrianism
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = traditionalist_zoroastrianism
				duration = -1
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = traditionalist_zoroastrianism
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
					religion = zoroastrian
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.6
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = same_doctrine_fanatical
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.2
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = same_doctrine_pious
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = -0.2
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = same_doctrine_observant
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = progressive_zoroastrianism
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = progressive_zoroastrianism
				duration = -1
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = progressive_zoroastrianism
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
					religion = zoroastrian
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.6
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = same_doctrine_fanatical
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.2
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = same_doctrine_pious
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = -0.2
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = same_doctrine_observant
					}
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = restorationist_zoroastrianism
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = restorationist_zoroastrianism
				duration = -1
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					has_country_modifier = restorationist_zoroastrianism
					NOT = {
						tag = ROOT
					}
					religion = zoroastrian
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.6
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = same_doctrine_fanatical
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = 0.2
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = same_doctrine_pious
					}
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						piety = -0.2
					}
					add_opinion = {
						who = ROOT
						modifier = same_doctrine_observant
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

				add_devotion = -20
				add_republican_tradition = -5
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
				add_legitimacy = -8
				add_devotion = -16
				add_republican_tradition = -4
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				add_legitimacy = -6
				add_devotion = -12
				add_republican_tradition = -3
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				add_legitimacy = -4
				add_devotion = -8
				add_republican_tradition = -2
			}
			else = {
				add_legitimacy = -2
				add_devotion = -4
				add_republican_tradition = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = caste_system_strict
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
				add_legitimacy = -5
				add_devotion = -10
				add_republican_tradition = -2.5
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
				add_legitimacy = -4
				add_devotion = -8
				add_republican_tradition = -2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				add_legitimacy = -3
				add_devotion = -6
				add_republican_tradition = -1.5
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				add_legitimacy = -2
				add_devotion = -4
				add_republican_tradition = -1
			}
			else = {
				add_legitimacy = -1
				add_devotion = -2
				add_republican_tradition = -0.5
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = caste_system_loose
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.60
				}
				add_legitimacy = -2.5
				add_devotion = -5
				add_republican_tradition = -1.25
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = 0.20
				}
				add_legitimacy = -2
				add_devotion = -4
				add_republican_tradition = -1
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.20
				}
				add_legitimacy = -1.5
				add_devotion = -3
				add_republican_tradition = -0.75
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					piety = -0.60
				}
				add_legitimacy = -1
				add_devotion = -2
				add_republican_tradition = -0.5
			}
			else = {
				add_legitimacy = -0.5
				add_devotion = -1
				add_republican_tradition = -0.25
			}
		}
		remove_country_modifier = caste_system_harsh
		remove_country_modifier = caste_system_strict
		remove_country_modifier = caste_system_loose
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = caste_system_relaxed
			duration = -1
		}
	}

						patriarch_corrupt_fanatical = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_fanatical
						}
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = patriarch_corrupt_observant
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				trigger_switch = {
					on_trigger = has_country_modifier
					patriarch_corrupt_observant = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_observant
					}
					patriarch_corrupt_pious = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_pious
					}
					patriarch_corrupt_fanatical = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_fanatical
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			trigger_switch = {
				on_trigger = has_country_modifier
				patriarch_corrupt_observant = {
					remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_observant
				}
				patriarch_corrupt_pious = {
					remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_pious
				}
				patriarch_corrupt_fanatical = {
					remove_country_modifier = patriarch_corrupt_fanatical
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = patriarch_hostile
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					patriarch_authority = 0.75
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
						}
					}
					trigger_switch = {
						on_trigger = has_country_modifier
						patriarch_hostile_observant = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
						}
						patriarch_hostile_pious = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
						}
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					patriarch_authority = 0.50
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
						}
					}
					trigger_switch = {
						on_trigger = has_country_modifier
						patriarch_hostile_observant = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
						}
						patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
						}
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = patriarch_hostile_pious
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					patriarch_authority = 0.10
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							has_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
						}
					}
					trigger_switch = {
						on_trigger = has_country_modifier
						patriarch_hostile_pious = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
						}
						patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {
							remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
						}
					}
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = patriarch_hostile_observant
						duration = -1
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				trigger_switch = {
					on_trigger = has_country_modifier
					patriarch_hostile_observant = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
					}
					patriarch_hostile_pious = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
					}
					patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {
						remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			trigger_switch = {
				on_trigger = has_country_modifier
				patriarch_hostile_observant = {
					remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_observant
				}
				patriarch_hostile_pious = {
					remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_pious
				}
				patriarch_hostile_fanatical = {
					remove_country_modifier = patriarch_hostile_fanatical
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
country_event = {
	id = dg_zoroastrian.078
	title = dg_zoroastrian.078.t
	desc = dg_zoroastrian.078.d
	picture = zoroastrian_religion
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = zoroastrian_rivayats_collected
	}
	option = {
		name = dg_zoroastrian.078.a
		remove_country_modifier = religious_controversy
		if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.60
			}
			add_prestige = 15
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = 0.20
			}
			add_prestige = 12
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.20
			}
			add_prestige = 9
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				piety = -0.60
			}
			add_prestige = 6
		}
		else = {
			add_prestige = 3
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				which = zoroastrian_rivayats
				value = 0
			}
		}
	}
}
